--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2022-01-25 04:28:54.000000000) ---
Patch Set 2:

Does this hurt performance more than needed if we flush the client page cache every time the layout lock is cancelled?  I think this would have less impact if the object OST DLM locks are cancelled only when the components are makred stale.

No clients should be using those objects, and this doesn't impact normal usage of the non-stale objects, and doesn't add overhead on the clients for checking the layout state for each page.

That isn't to say I'm against it, if this is how we can fix the problem right now, but I think it could be better.  We should test the performance impact of this patch, if any, and maybe it isn't as much impact as I think.

--- Message (Alex Zhuravlev, 2022-01-25 05:40:45.000000000) ---
Patch Set 2:

it doesn't really flush pagecache, but it force llite to go regular way: revalidate layout lock, fetch layout, select object to read, etc.

--- Message (Alex Zhuravlev, 2022-01-25 05:45:40.000000000) ---
Patch Set 2:

i'll try to make a test to verify that pagecache still can be used after layout revalidation.

--- Message (Patrick Farrell, 2022-04-12 15:35:53.000000000) ---
Patch Set 10:

Alex,

The problem is real of course, but I agree with Shadow’s implied question.

Why isn’t the page removed by conf_set?  Shouldn’t it be?  Checking the layout version works in the test but I’m not sure we should have to do it.  (I’m also not sure locking on layout version changes is enough to keep this safe.)

--- Message (Alexey Lyashkov, 2022-04-12 19:06:26.000000000) ---
Patch Set 10:

Alex,

I don't say "problem isn't real" but solution looks strange. Once layout can changed during generic_file_read_iter call. Page should be have clear up2date flag (in case MM hold a last reference), or page should unlinked from mapping (if no extra references).

--- Message (Alex Zhuravlev, 2022-04-12 20:18:46.000000000) ---
Patch Set 10:

(1) ll_conf_set(OBJECT_CONF_INVALIDATE) -> vvp_conf_set() -- this codepath does not invalidate cache pages
(2) IMO the reason do not invalidate pages is clear - a layout change doesn't mean data change. for example, when a new compoenent is being added. why this should cause page invalidation for the pages which are to stay?

--- Message (Alexey Lyashkov, 2022-04-13 08:55:34.000000000) ---
Patch Set 10:

because this may a result of layout swap and client don't control an data placement now?

--- Message (Alex Zhuravlev, 2022-04-13 08:59:39.000000000) ---
Patch Set 10:

I'd say a bit different: because the client doesn't check the layout on the fast path. page invalidation as a reaction to a lost layout lock looks too heavy to me. extra ldlm lock match on every read would be painful for fast reads, I guess. so here is the compromise.

--- Message (Alexey Lyashkov, 2022-04-13 09:22:42.000000000) ---
Patch Set 10:

well, let me run our reproducer to see a better solution.

--- Message (Alexey Lyashkov, 2022-04-13 13:00:18.000000000) ---
Patch Set 10:

looking in our test - it have a write a data to primary replica - so it good place to flush data from page cache. With normal file - it should caused a lock cancel and flush a data from page cache.
I don't understand why you think it should be different in mirror case?

--- Message (Alexey Lyashkov, 2022-04-13 13:30:03.000000000) ---
Patch Set 10:

in other view, once page don't unlinked and uptodate isn't clear - this page may read via mmap I think :/ which don't covers this fix.

--- Message (Alex Zhuravlev, 2022-04-15 18:54:59.000000000) ---
Patch Set 10:

I guess it makes sense to check how mmap is actually handleded, but vvp_conf_set() has this code:
                /* Clean up page mmap for this inode.
                 * The reason for us to do this is that if the page has
                 * already been installed into memory space, the process
                 * can access it without interacting with lustre, so this
                 * page may be stale due to layout change, and the process
                 * will never be notified.
                 * This operation is expensive but mmap processes have to pay
                 * a price themselves. */
                unmap_mapping_range(conf->coc_inode->i_mapping,
                                    0, OBD_OBJECT_EOF, 0);
